Women's World Idleness Bi Yao Often reported in newspapers: In many places in the country, this village has killed people, and the dogs in that village smell the blood and lose their guarding duties, vying to lick the heads and blood of people. The old men, seeing this abnormal behavior of animals, only think that the way of heaven has changed, and they are frightened and amazed.

In fact, there is nothing to be frightened about. Aren't the villages there all bare? Being a dog is also very boring, so naturally they go to places with trumpets and bloodshed to relieve their boredom. This is the norm of animal nature.

No matter what it is, when it gets too idle, it likes strange and novel tastes. The reason why patients want to eat this and that in bed is the same.

Over the years, the whole country has been desperately focused on women, is there really something big about women? It's just picking up this strange taste to cure their idleness. Therefore, all events involving young women will cause a city-wide uproar. Just look at the recent "Jinan Scandal," how sensational it is!

"(Jinan Express) The sensational Jinan Education Department instructor Zhou Guangyan, whose wife, a female normal school student Wang Zhixian, was seduced and eloped by Wang Chongfan, an employee of the arsenal, causing a scandal. All civil servants in the province were unanimously indignant and planned to ask Governor Han Fuqu to strictly pursue... Unexpectedly, Wang and others were arrested on the 4th of this month in Liuhe County, north of the capital of Jiangsu Province. After the news spread to Shandong, the once silent scandal became very active in society, and the atmosphere suddenly became tense. All parties still unanimously advocate strict punishment.

In addition, there are also many letters from young students from various places to comfort Zhou Guangyan, and many people offer ideas on Zhou's behalf. Looking back since June 1st, no one in the Pingjin area has not been sweating from the summer heat; while in the Qilu area, it is warm and people are overturned for peach blossoms, indignant for peach blossoms, and tense for peach blossoms. With just a river separating them, the north and south are so different!

Does the combination or separation of a pair of men and women among the 400 million people have even a hair's worth of impact on others? But the social people, even the civil servants who have the responsibility to defend the territory and protect the people, are moved to public anger for this. It should be clear that they are "idle." Everyone suffers from idleness, arguing over private matters between men and women, how can the affairs of the country be not so impressive?

The source of idleness, some is stolen by oneself, some is given by others. Those who love themselves will certainly not steal idleness, but at the same time, they will not guard the idleness given by others. The dogs that run from the countryside to other villages to lick blood are given a deserted and idle place by the people in chaos; dogs are animals, unable to compete with humans, and they can be content with that position. If even the people in the sub-colonial territories who cannot steal idleness are still mired in "idleness" and cannot extricate themselves, then what kind of thing are they comparing themselves to?

We don't want to see women who are so idle that they fall into the web of love like drunkards, staging peach blossom incidents beyond reason like Liu Lu. We also don't want to see men suffering from "idleness," only knowing to sniff women with sharp noses, constantly playing peach blossom incidents or being nervous for others' peach blossom incidents. Because the current society is male-centered, they bear the majority of the responsibility for all the evils that cause society and the country to sink and perish. Women's Issues Lecture, Section 4: The French Revolution and Women Jun Hui

The current capitalist society is certainly not something that suddenly appeared. It has gone through various stages of development, and it must go through the firm struggle of the industrial and commercial citizens to be realized. This stage of development can be divided into three. Namely, the First Religious Revolution (1517), the Second English Revolution (1688), and the Third is the French Revolution in which the industrial and commercial citizens finally gained political power.

The French Revolution gave a great influence on the women's liberation movement and thought. This influence is most fully expressed in the famous Declaration of the Rights of Man. Under the feudal absolute monarchy, all common people completely lost their status as "humans," not to mention that women were destined to be slaves. A small number of feudal special people arbitrarily extracted the blood and sweat of the masses, doing whatever they wanted, living a life of paradise on earth, while the majority of people engaged in production, especially women, suffered the pain of hell in this world. Under this status quo, the bourgeoisie rose up! Holding up the flags of freedom, equality, and fraternity, they declared the rights of the people and attacked the feudal forces. Their flags and their claims were righteous and justified. Therefore, the workers and peasants who had suffered from oppression for years enthusiastically participated in the revolutionary ranks, and the most oppressed women bravely participated in the rebellion of the masses. As a result, the autocratic kingdom was overthrown, and the industrial and commercial citizens seized power and established a new government. However, the workers and peasants and women who directly shed blood did not get any rights. Instead, they suffered from the suppression and massacre of the new government! They only replaced the old oppressor with a new target of oppression.

Nevertheless, the French Revolution marked an important stage of evolution in history. From then on, human material and spiritual civilization has not been subject to any restrictions and has developed rapidly, thus creating a brilliant modern culture.

The Declaration of the Rights of Man in the French Revolution and the American Declaration of Independence (1776) are epoch-making documents with profound significance in the history of human liberation. It not only expresses the demands of all oppressed people, but also gives a very profound and powerful hint to the masses of women who have long lost their human rights. The Declaration of Independence states: "All men are created equal, endowed with certain unalienable rights, among which are life, liberty, and the pursuit of happiness." Government is instituted to protect these rights, deriving its powers from the consent of the governed. The Declaration of the Rights of Man also contains the following claims: "Article 1: Men are born and remain free and equal in rights. Social distinctions may be founded only upon the general good. Article 2: The aim of all political association is the preservation of the natural and imprescriptible rights of man." Although it does not specifically point out the rights of women, since women are a part of humanity, they naturally have the right to obtain the same freedom and equality as men. Although bourgeois society did not give women any rights after the American War of Independence and the French Revolution, the above two declarations did indeed become the main opportunity for women to begin to demand all human rights.

At the time of the French Revolution, on the one hand, a large number of knowledgeable women who had fully absorbed modern liberal ideas had emerged among the industrial and commercial women. On the other hand, with the expansion of industrial production, the number of female workers in major cities, especially in Paris and Marseille, increased alarmingly. These two types of women formed the main combat force in the revolutionary rebellion. According to historical records, the female workers of Paris participated in the struggle to occupy the Bastille prison. The female workers were led by Rosa Lacombe, Madeleine Chabry, and Lénardoux, and organized the Versailles attack team. Of particular interest is the escort of Louis XVI to Paris by the Women's Guard.

There were two main female leaders in the French Revolution, one was Theroigne de Mericourt and the other was Lacombe. Theroigne de Mericourt had a passionate fighting character. She led the crowd to occupy the Bastille prison, so the National Assembly awarded her a sword of honor in recognition of her. On October 5th, the day of the attack on Versailles, she wore a red dress and rode a horse to attack Versailles in support of the revolutionary spirit of the women. On August 10th, in order to defend the Republican government, she gave speeches all night in the square, demanding the establishment of the true supreme power of the people.

Lacombe was also a woman who participated in the Versailles march. She was the true leader of the working women in the suburbs of Paris. She often lived with the lower-class women. She was a woman with outstanding organizational skills, beautiful voice, and appearance. She shouted from the auditorium of the Legislative Assembly: "Defend the revolution from the invasion of the Allied forces!" At the same time, she demanded "popularization of power." When attacking the palace on August 10th, her arm was injured. The National Assembly specially awarded her the glorious "Civic Crown." She founded the "Revolutionary Women's Club" to educate the masses of women with the spirit of revolution. She was a famous eloquent female Jacobin member. She not only advocated the rights of women, but also demanded the interests of the masses of women. She shouted:

"What benefits have women received under the Republican system!"

It can be seen that the women's movement is being cared for by people. It is planned to disclose the main points in the next issue for public discussion. Please pay special attention to readers. Girls Living a Mouse Life Qian Since being responsible in the small building on Street Mi and recognizing the deformed society in this area, there have been two sounds that knock on my eardrums and make me tremble uncontrollably. That is the sound of the patrol car's horn and the "beep" of the Western machine foot road car.

This street was a graveyard of ghosts eight years ago. Since the outbreak of the January 28th Incident, it has begun to expand and develop until today. Its position of prosperity is about to catch up with the intersection of Annam Road and Hede Road. The morning vegetable market here is very bustling and noisy. The vegetable market is a temporary vegetable market where many vegetable vendors set up stalls along the street every morning. In addition to the stalls connected one after another in front of people's doors, there are countless vegetable vendors carrying one or two baskets or carrying two baskets selling while walking and shouting. Among these vegetable vendors, women, especially young girls, are the majority. Nine out of ten of them do not have public hawker permits.

We Chinese people, living in the concessions leased by imperialists, which should have been our own territory, cannot live in houses unless we pay house donations, and cars cannot pass through without paying car donations. If you want to do business, you can't even think about making a living without a business permit. These young girls selling vegetables have no license to do business in the concession, but they want to make a living in the concession, so their business situation is completely secretive, like mice. Every time they stop a customer, they always look around left and right, look forward and backward, to see if there is any danger of patrolmen coming. If they don't see any, they slowly haggle over the price of the vegetables (according to the general situation, the vegetables sold by these vendors are cheaper than those in the vegetable stalls), but if they catch sight of a patrolman from afar, they casually take some money and run to the attached alley or lane. In this situation, they often don't have time to collect the money, pick up the basket or shoulder the burden and run away. At this time, the customers who have already put the vegetables in their own baskets, those with cruel hearts, often take the opportunity to rob them, picking up the basket and leaving. After the patrolmen pass, those vegetable-selling girls who have suffered losses have to admit their bad luck.

This wonderful scene of the patrolmen chasing unlicensed vegetable vendors is the most fierce at nine or ten o'clock in the morning. At that time, the vegetable market is booming, and the streets are crowded with vegetable vendors and buyers. Looking up, you can see nothing but black heads, like a big river full of watermelons. Suddenly, without everyone knowing, a patrol car stopped from afar. Several Western and Chinese patrolmen got out of the car. Soon, there will be a big commotion in the vegetable market. Those vegetable vendors without permits are really scared and run around with their heads in their hands. As a result, the car always carries five or six unfortunate people away every morning. When the car drives away with its unique horn, my heart will sink in my body.

According to a vegetable-selling girl, the first time they go to the police station to register to sell vegetables, they need seven silver dollars, and then they need to pay two silver dollars every month to renew the permit. If they are taken to the police station without a permit, they will be fined five cents each time. If they have no money, they will be jailed for a day. As for their daily business, they can sell at most one thousand copper coins. In good times, they can earn three or four hundred cash. In bad times, two or three hundred or one or two hundred cash is uncertain. In this way, all their earnings for five or six days are not enough to pay for one penalty, let alone buy a permit. Besides, they have to buy something to survive every day. This is why they live a mouse life.

And this kind of vegetable-selling girl living such a life – a mouse life – there are also peddlers who sell snacks all day long on the streets. Recently, there are more and more such peddlers on the streets every day. They are all young girls who have not been in the city for long from the countryside. You can tell this just by looking at the red hair ropes on their upturned braids and the rural atmosphere all over them. The items they sell change with the seasons. When the weather is not hot, they sell chestnuts, and then gradually change to sugar plums, Shandong loquats. Now they are selling big sweet peaches. Although the police station does not have special cars to take them away in batches at noon and afternoon, Western patrolmen riding machine foot road cars and Chinese patrolmen riding ordinary bicycles come to patrol the streets every hour. When they chase, they chase in cars. Poor these yellow-haired girls have to train their vision and hearing to be as sharp as mice in order to live and save their lives. When they run, they really have to kick their hooves and fly.

One day, a thirteen or fourteen-year-old girl peddler, carrying a basket of loquats, ran desperately into the alley next door. When I rushed down to see, she was lying crookedly next to the refuse bin like a dead rat, her face pale, and she was still muttering hysterically, "Oh, here they come! Oh, here they come!" At this time, my eyes immediately saw clearly that Zhao Liujia, the vegetable-selling girl who was chased and beaten to death by the Western patrolmen not long ago, was here. And I saw even more clearly that these poor girls who cannot afford permits but have to make a living in the tiger's mouth have the possibility of dying tragically like this every day.

The Shanghai Women's Society's Girls' Association is discussing the health problems of girls in the parks of the foreign masters, asking girls to pay attention to exercise and swimming. I think the healthy and beautiful bodies of those girls in the greenhouse will not be used to escape the claws of the imperialists like these girls living a mouse life, will they? Mom's Days Yingzi He, the father of the child, he hates children the most. When the child was born, he was ready to send her to the nursery. I refused. In such a dangerous society, if a girl is abandoned, what will her future be like? I would rather throw her into the Huangpu River than let her be humiliated and suffer in the future. As long as we can barely survive, which mother would be willing to abandon her children? He often said: What do you want her for? We are still young, are we afraid of not having children in the future? I can't support her. I can't be a beast of burden for you and the child, ruin myself, sell myself. A person should plan for a career, for life, for our happiness, the only way is to send her away. Whenever the child cried, he would mutter this long speech.

"Crying is his language, don't you allow him to cry? Children always cry..."

"I hate crying, I can't support her, it's not a crime to send her away, right! You see, I'll send her to the nursery tomorrow. You're not allowed to make noise. If you love me, you have to listen to me..." He looked at me with stern eyes, as if a judge was waiting for a prisoner's answer.

"Okay; do as you please, please rest in peace! Don't make noise, there are many classes tomorrow." I answered him, suppressing the anger in my stomach,

Around nine o'clock the next day, he really sent the child to the nursery. After the child was taken away, I cried, crying very sadly. I have never been a person who cries and doesn't shed tears. This time, there were more tears than spring rain? Through the efforts of friends, after spending four dollars in handling fees, the child was still brought back. How happy I am! Before the child was brought back, my heart was always beating. I was always afraid of being taken away by others. I didn't even know why. It seems that as soon as a child is born, there is an indestructible emotion with the mother. I think maternal love is the purest and most sincere. Before I became a mother, I didn't feel that maternal love was so great. Before, when I saw many children being very fierce to their mothers, I thought to myself, why don't you kill such a son? Now I know that there is no mother who does not love her children, no matter how bad the children are to her, she will understand and still love them!

Mother, my mother far away across the mountains and rivers, when holding your grandson, I will think of how you raised us sisters in the past. I am very sad and ashamed, mother: you are already old, you have already entered the twilight years with disheveled white hair, and you still often worry about your daughter who is drifting far away. What comfort does she have for you?

May 23rd These few days, I have been very troubled in my heart. The child is noisy and crying, and I feel even more sad. I wish I could give her a good beating, but what does such a small child know?

Arguing with his father for the sake of the child has also become commonplace. When the child cries, he insists on sending her to someone else's house, saying that he can't support her,

"Go find a lady who doesn't have children: otherwise, you can be a monk," I was so angry with him, I felt he was too selfish. He saw that I liked the child and was afraid that I would be indifferent to him. I don't know if every young father is like this.

"I, I always want her to be able to live on her own,"

"Who doesn't want to live on their own, who wants to fall? When the child is weaned, I will go to work. I don't have knowledge, but I have a healthy body, so I can always work,"

"Isn't it good to send this foot-binding ghost away? Go exercise yourself, for your future"

"If you want to send her away, first discuss it with your father. If they all say to send her away, I will send her away"

"This is a matter between the two of us, why ask them? Will he support you for the rest of your life in the future?"

"My God, you don't understand me at all, who wants to rely on others..."

What's the use of arguing? It will only damage our feelings. Now I have changed my attitude. When he talks about these things, I will talk about something else. When the child is older, I will live my own life! Legal Q&A Xing Yingming asks: I married Mr. Zhang in the first year of Xuantong. My father (who is still alive) has a lot of wealth: but he is stubborn and values ​​sons over daughters. I have twelve siblings in total. Now because the population is growing day by day, there is a proposal to divide the family. However, I was not included, which is very surprising. However, because I don't have legal knowledge, I have no confidence to negotiate with him. I have a few questions, and I hope Mr. can teach me: (1) Do I have the right to be divided? (2) Is it against the law if my father is unwilling to give it to me? And can I legally request a division? (3) If he currently owes some debts, will I be obligated to repay them if I receive property? (Answer) The inheritance of this case has not yet begun. (According to the inheritance, it begins when the deceased dies.) Your father is making a gift because the children are dividing the family, and he is legally free to do so. Also, because the inheritance has not yet begun, the lady has no obligation to repay the debts owed by your father. Because lifetime gifts are different from estate analysis. (Answered by lawyer Pu Shunqing)

Special Telecommunications Edition Voice of the Telecommunications Industry Recent Major Reforms in the Telecommunications Administration Organization De The biggest shortcomings in my country's telecommunications administration organization are (1) Ununified business, (2) Ununified engineering. Regarding the problem of telegraph business, fortunately, our authorities have adhered to the spirit of courageously advancing and worked hard, and were able to merge the local bureaus and stations in order, and since April of this year, the Qingdao, Jinan, Xiamen, Wanxian, Fuzhou, Yantai, Changsha and other bureaus and stations have wireless telegraph rooms, and the work of relocation and merger in one place has been implemented. Not only is the management convenient, but also the transmission speed is increased. As for the telephone business problem, in the past, the long-distance telephones in each province were managed by the telephone operators of each line (for example, the telephone operators of long-distance telephones such as Jiqing, Jinghu, etc.) were responsible for the jurisdiction. Then it was renamed as the long-distance telephone operators of each province. It was not until April of this year that the Long-Distance Telephone Administration Bureau was merged into the Telecommunications Administration Bureau, and the original operators were still in charge of long-distance telephone affairs. Since then, the business of reporting and telephone in the entire region has been under the unified command of the Administration Bureau. Needless to say, it is helpful to the development of the telecommunications business. This is one of the major reforms in my country's telecommunications administration organization. Secondly, regarding the engineering problem: it is found that although the long-distance telephone business is under the jurisdiction of the Administration Bureau, the maintenance and maintenance of the trunk and branch lines are still the responsibility of the Trunk Line Engineering Office and the Engineering Section of the Administration Bureau respectively. Not only is it difficult to divide the duties of the chief engineer and the director of engineering, but also the organization inevitably has the drawbacks of overlapping beds and houses. Now the Ministry of Communications resolutely merges all the trunk line engineering offices into the Administration Bureau, and all duties are completely the responsibility of the Engineering Section of the Administration Bureau. And it is stipulated to be implemented from July 1st of this year. From then on, whether it is trunk line, engineering, or branch line engineering, it is under the unified control of the Administration Bureau, and the authority has been concentrated, and the expenses have been reduced. This is the second major reform in my telecommunications administration organization. What is more, recently, the telegraph and telephone bureaus in Wuxian and Zhenjiang have been merged. The importance of the language number is really no less than the above two reforms. The reporter hopes that our authorities will continue to implement their proposals and merge the local telephone bureaus and report bureaus in order to exert the highest efficiency in administration. The Relationship between the Gold Franc and International Telegraphs Yuncheng The telegrams between China and foreign countries are called international telegrams. The fees and various handling procedures for this kind of telegrams must be handled in accordance with the International Telecommunication Convention and the attached telegraph rules jointly established by more than 70 countries around the world. Article 32 of the Convention states that the price of international telegrams should be based on the gold franc. The so-called gold franc is a hypothetical currency with a total weight of 10/31 of a gram and a gold content of 900/1000. According to this calculation, its value is about five times that of the French franc currently in actual use. Before the gold price fell in mid-January of this year, one French franc was worth about two jiao of our country's silver dollars, so one gold franc was worth about one yuan of our country's silver dollars. Later, the gold price gradually fell, and the value of the French franc decreased from two jiao to one jiao nine fen, one jiao eight fen... All the values of the gold franc also decreased to nine jiao four fen, nine jiao... of silver dollars accordingly. From the above, we know that the price of international telegrams is based on the gold franc, not the national currency silver dollar. This is the big difference between international telegrams and domestic telegrams, and it is also the reason why international telegrams are expensive. To give an example, the price of sending a telegram from China to the United Kingdom in the spring of the 19th year of the Republic of China was 3.75 gold francs per word (one franc is equal to one hundred centimes), while the price in the spring of this year was 3.45 gold francs, which was 30 centimes lower than that of the year. However, the value of the gold franc in the spring of the 19th year of the Republic of China was five jiao of the national currency, so 3.75 francs only amounted to one yuan, eight jiao, seven fen and five li of the national currency, while the value of the gold franc in the spring of this year was one yuan of the national currency, so 3.45 francs must amount to two yuan, four jiao and five fen of the national currency, which is one yuan, five jiao and seven fen and five li higher than that of the spring of the 19th year. The situation of sending telegrams to other countries is also the same. In short, in recent years, although the Ministry of Communications has tried its best to lower the price of telegrams sent from my country to foreign countries, because of the relationship between gold price and exchange rate, the burden on the senders has increased instead of decreasing, which is really a helpless thing. Since January of this year, the silver price has been rising and the gold price has been falling. Although the pros and cons of this matter for my country's entire industry, commerce and finance are another issue, at least to a limited extent, the value of the gold franc has fallen accordingly. At the beginning of this year, the value of one gold franc was still one yuan of the national currency, but it was reduced to nine jiao and five fen on March 1st, and recently it was reduced to eight jiao and seven fen from June 1st, so the cost of international telegrams has been reduced by no less than 13% in half a year. This point is welcomed by the Ministry of Communications and the public who send international telegrams all over the country. Because on the one hand, the burden of telegram fees can be reduced for the senders of international telegrams, and on the other hand, although the telegram fee per word received by the Ministry of Communications for international telegrams has been reduced, it is hoped that the business will be more developed in the future. If the gold price continues to fall in the future, then the price of international telegrams can also be reduced! Silver Issues and Telecommunications Hao Since the United States raised the silver price, the drastic changes in the Sino-US exchange rate have been unprecedented. As a result, the silver price has skyrocketed and silver has flowed out, forming the tragic phenomenon of extreme financial panic at present. The recent cause is due to the increase in the silver price in the United States, and tracing the root cause should be attributed to the imbalance of international trade over the years. This can be seen in Mr. Ma Yinchu's recent article "Opinions on the Silver Problem." Mr. Ma said: "To protect the domestic silver, the only way is to balance international trade and solve the trade deficit. The trade deficit is the root cause of the current silver outflow, and the way to prevent the current silver outflow should be sought from this root cause, which has become a consensus of the whole country. Therefore, when it comes to China's silver problem, the conclusion must be transformed from the silver problem to the foreign trade problem." Mr. Ma's words are incisive and simple. Reducing imports and increasing exports is the only way to prevent the outflow of silver, and it is also the only way to fundamentally solve our country's economic panic. We deeply feel that the reason for the annual outflow of silver is that the purchase of telecommunications equipment and the sending of international telegrams are also considerable. Since the establishment of telecommunications, it has been more than 50 years, and all the main materials required have not yet been manufactured by ourselves, and we still have to rely on foreigners. According to the survey, the cost of purchasing this item by the Ministry of Communications is about 5 million yuan per year, and other expansion materials are not included. If the telecommunications equipment used in various provinces is included, the number is astonishing. As for the international telegram fees, because our country did not have self-operated and independent agencies for foreign communications in the past, all kinds of telegrams sent to foreign countries were transmitted by the water line company, so the international telegram fees in the whole country. About 8 million yuan per year fell into the hands of foreigners, and in the past 50 years, it has not been less than 400 million yuan. These two huge expenditures are nothing but good silver, and we watch it flow out without return, isn't it heartbreaking! Although, the telecommunications industry colleagues are not unable to manufacture various telecommunications equipment, but the strength is not enough, because the establishment of a telecommunications equipment factory requires a huge amount of money. Judging from the past telecommunications book revenue figures, it seems easy to handle this matter. However, the bulk of this number is occupied by the long-overdue military officer telegraph fees. Not to mention the remote ones, but from the military officer telegraph fees accumulated by the national military and political agencies since the establishment of the National Government to the end of the 23rd year, it has reached the huge amount of 22,106,510.0905 yuan. The telecommunications economy has been hit by this, and the plan to manufacture telecommunications equipment by itself cannot be put into practice! As a result, the principle of self-sufficiency has not been achieved, and the outflow of silver will never end. It is not an exaggeration to say that the military officer's telegraph arrears indirectly caused the outflow of silver in the telecommunications sector. As for the international lightning reports, since the Ministry of Communications established the International Radio Station in the 18th year, the leakage has gradually been recovered. Since this year, the internal equipment of the station has been expanded and improved, and the direct circuits have also been increased at the same time, so the business situation has progressed year by year. Recently, the monthly report fee income of the station has exceeded 400,000 yuan. In other words, the outflow of silver can be reduced by 5 million yuan per year. What are the disadvantages of silver outflow? There are serious and obvious facts presented before our eyes. We are suffering, it is really in deep water. Only by learning from the past and unifying from top to bottom can we try our best to find ways to prevent the outflow of silver from all aspects. At this time, we would like to sincerely point out two things we hope for: First, our telecommunications authorities and telecommunications colleagues are determined to seek self-sufficiency in telecommunications equipment, but because of economic difficulties, they are unable to do so, and the biggest reason for economic difficulties is due to the accumulation of military officer's telegraph fees. The military officer's telegraph fees are like a drop in the ocean compared to the entire military salary and political expenses, and the amount is extremely small. Mr. Zuo Jun has earnestly said in his article "The Future of Sichuan and Guizhou Telecommunications" in the 37th issue of this journal. We hope that our wise military and political authorities will understand the difficulties of telecommunications and strive to pay the report fees, then the telecommunications equipment in the future will have the possibility of being manufactured by ourselves, and the international situation is unpredictable. Once a war breaks out, the source of materials will be cut off, and the entire telecommunications traffic will inevitably be unable to maintain, which will have a huge impact on the future of national defense. Therefore, for the sake of national defense and transportation, we should plan for it early. And the way to plan is to enrich the telecommunications economy, and the way to enrich is to pay the military officer's telegraph fees. Second, although the international telegram fee has recovered about 400,000 yuan per month, the entire international telegram fee in the country is about 800,000 yuan to 900,000 yuan per month. The international radio station has only recovered half of it, and the other half is still obtained by foreigners. We sincerely hope that our patriotic people will be aware of the suffering imposed on us by the outflow of silver and deeply reflect on it. In the future, when sending international telegrams, they will unanimously specify that they be transmitted through wireless circuits that are fast, accurate, and economical, so as to protect national treasures and fulfill the national duty! A Message to the Highway Construction Authorities Hua Please Maintain the Telegraph Pole Lines The transmission of wired telecommunications must rely on the medium of conductors to reach from one end to the other. Therefore, any part of the conductor that has an obstacle will inevitably lead to the disruption of current and communication. The way to maintain it is to cooperate with each other. The maintenance and repair of the mechanical wiring installed indoors is certainly very easy. As for the overhead pole lines that stand in the wilderness, it is difficult to protect and maintain them due to the excessive distance. The Ministry of Communications has always made its greatest efforts to maintain the pole lines in order to avoid various man-made and natural infringements. For example, it has approved the Executive Yuan to formulate the rules for the maintenance of state-owned telegraph and telephone pole lines to prevent bandits from destroying them; it has banned the flying of kites near the power lines to avoid the entanglement of the power lines. It has sent workers to wipe the dust from the insulators to avoid leakage of the lines. All telecommunications bureaus that manage the lines must also conduct tests every morning to find out where the line problems are and know how to prevent them. If an obstacle occurs, workers will be sent immediately to repair it to minimize the time of communication disruption. However, this effort by the Ministry of Communications will be useless if any related party does not cooperate with it. The fact that telecommunications pole lines in various places have been damaged by road construction workers for no reason in recent years is one example. We all know that the opening of highways is generally very urgent. In order to speed up the construction, fires are often set to burn mountains and rocks, or explosives are used to blow them up. The telecommunications pole lines along the way will inevitably suffer. In addition, the workers who build highways are mostly recruited temporarily and have not been trained. They do not know how to maintain the pole lines along the way, and they often damage them for no reason during construction, considering it a common occurrence. If there is sufficient preparation in advance, it seems not difficult to find a way to solve it. When surveying the highway route, if the impact on the telecommunications pole lines along the way is taken into account, it can be moved and avoided immediately. If the road construction workers are given a little instruction in advance, they will not damage it for no reason and hinder communication. How can this be done by the highway authorities? The problem is extremely simple. Both telecommunications and highways are related to national defense. The close relationship between them is like the interdependence of lips and teeth. Without telecommunications equipment on highways, all construction progress and long-distance driving will experience great difficulties. Without the assistance of highways, it is difficult to survey and repair telecommunications pole lines. The Ministry of Communications has always supported the construction of highways in various provinces. For example, it has an agreement with the National Economic Commission on the cooperation of telephone on the Xilan Highway. It stipulates that when the long-distance car operating agency on the road uses long-distance telephones, it can pay half the usual fee. In order to facilitate the communication of long-distance cars in case of obstacles or temporary emergencies, anyone with a temporary telephone on the car can hook up and connect to the nearest station for communication in the middle. In order to facilitate the sending of telegrams by the engineering team, a telegraph operator is specially assigned to carry telegraph and telephone equipment and application materials to set up a temporary reporting room at the location of the engineering team. All of these are the actual manifestations of the Ministry of Communications' support for highway construction. We firmly believe that the highway authorities all over the country are committed to developing domestic transportation and must have the same view on the maintenance of telecommunications pole lines. If they can give practical and effective cooperation to solve the difficulties that the Ministry of Communications has encountered in the past, then it will be a blessing for telecommunications, and it is also what the reporter hopes for. Implementation of Industrial and Commercial Lending: Guarantee Loan Committee Established; Cai Zengji Elected Chairman; Direct Loans from Banks and Money Shops; Money Industry Loan Syndicate Approves Cash Collateral 154

Xin Xin News reports: The Ministry of Finance, to implement the relief of industry and commerce, appointed Cai Zengji as chairman, Du Yuesheng and Wu Xingya as deputy chairmen, and Chen Guangfu and three others as committee members. Banks and money shops decided to maximize lending to relieve industry and commerce. Details as follows:

Guarantee Loan Committee Established

The Ministry of Finance allocated 2,000 yuan in national treasury certificates, instructing Cai Zengji and others to receive and safeguard them, to serve as a secondary guarantee for banks and money shops to provide industrial and commercial relief loans according to the ten principles promulgated by the Ministry of Finance. On the afternoon of the 14th, at 1:00 PM, Xu Kan, Vice Minister of Finance, convened all committee members at the Zhong You Tian Restaurant on Sanma Road to discuss implementation matters. Those present included Vice Minister Xu, Cai Zengji, Wu Xingya, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Chen Guangfu, Wang Yansong, Qin Runqing, Xi Demao, Zhang Peishen, Yu Zuoting, and Song Ziliang, totaling twelve people. Vice Minister Xu chaired the meeting, reporting that the purpose of this allocation of national treasury certificates was to provide relief loans to industry and commerce in the city, with banks and money shops directly providing the loans and the national treasury certificates serving as a secondary guarantee. The nature of this was purely a guarantee loan, not a loan account. After discussion, the following was decided: (1) Regarding the organization of the committee, there would be one chairman, two deputy chairmen, and four standing committee members. The above seven people would form the standing committee. (2) Cai Zengji was elected chairman, and Du Yuesheng and Wu Xingya were elected deputy chairmen. Chen Guangfu, Qin Runqing, Yu Zuoting, and Song Ziliang were elected standing committee members. (3) It was decided that on June 15th at 4:00 PM, a meeting would be held at the Bankers' Association to discuss the draft organizational charter prepared by the chairman. The meeting adjourned at around 3:00 PM.

Yesterday's Meeting Discussed the Charter

Xin Sheng News reports: After the establishment of the Industrial and Commercial Relief Guarantee Loan Committee, a committee meeting was held yesterday afternoon at 4:30 PM at the Bankers' Club on Hong Kong Road. The committee members present included Cai Zengji, Wu Xingya, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Chen Guangfu, Wang Yansong, Qin Runqing, Xi Demao, Zhang Peishen, Yu Zuoting, and Song Ziliang, totaling twelve people. Chairman Cai Zengji first reported on the proceedings of the first meeting on June 14th. Then, the draft charter of the Industrial and Commercial Relief Guarantee Loan Committee, prepared by the chairman, was discussed item by item, amended, and resolved. (1) After the chairman revises the draft, it will be submitted for approval at the meeting on June 17th at 2:00 PM. (2) The office will be temporarily located within the China National Goods Bank on Henan Road. The meeting adjourned at 6:30 PM.

National Goods Bank to Serve as Accountant

A reporter from Xin Sheng News learned from a committee member last night that the committee charter drafted by Chairman Cai Zengji is based on the ten principles promulgated by the Ministry of Finance. Factories manufacturing national goods and merchants selling national goods who wish to mortgage goods for loans may apply to the committee. After the committee reviews and approves the application, it will notify banks and money shops to provide the loans. The goods of the factories and merchants will serve as the first guarantee, and the national treasury certificates will serve as the second guarantee. All accounting matters will be handled by the China National Goods Bank.

Loan Syndicate Accepts Collateral

Xin Xin News reports: After the Ministry of Finance allocated the 24th year financial public bonds to relieve the money industry, money shops are submitting various deeds, public bonds, goods, and other collateral to the Money Industry Preparation Depository for review by the Money Industry Supervision Committee. According to Xin Xin News reporters, the supervision committee has completely reviewed all the collateral and calculated its value according to the prescribed pricing standards. Together with the previously reviewed 1,560,000 yuan, the total amounts to more than 24,460,000 yuan, which is only more than 240,000 yuan short of the 25 million yuan in financial public bonds. The various types of collateral approved by the Supervision Committee have also been approved by the Money Industry Loan Syndicate for acceptance as cash collateral.

Money Industry Loans Available for Withdrawal at Any Time

The more than 24,460,000 yuan in collateral from the money industry approved by the Supervision Committee has been accepted by the Money Industry Loan Syndicate as collateral for cash loans. As for the general loan methods, the Money Industry Joint Preparation Depository has notified all shops that they can withdraw funds from the syndicate at any time when needed. According to Xin Xin News reporters, as of 5:00 PM yesterday, only a small portion of the more than 24 million yuan in loans had been withdrawn. The banks and money shops are concentrating on centralized remittances. The results of daily settlements show that if a money shop needs to transfer funds to a bank, it will be deducted from the collateral.

Banks and Money Shops to Maximize Lending

The Shanghai money industry, due to the difficulties caused by remittance drawings, was relieved by the Ministry of Finance with the allocation of 25 million yuan in 24th year financial public bonds. After the implementation of centralized collection and resolution of remittance drafts between the two industries, the financial situation in southern Shanghai has stabilized. To maintain industry and commerce and revitalize the market, banks and money shops have now decided to maximize the provision of relief loans to industry and commerce. The Ministry of Finance has specifically allocated 20 million yuan in national treasury certificates as a secondary guarantee, while the collateral from factories and merchants serves as the first guarantee. Therefore, the repayment of principal is absolutely reliable, and both banks and money shops are happy to provide loans. As of the 15th, factories and merchants have submitted applications to the relevant National Goods Associations requesting loans amounting to more than 33 million yuan.

Yuan Liang Telegraphed Huang Fu Yesterday, Reporting That Peace and Tranquility in Beiping is As Usual 155

Huang Fu, Chairman of the Peiping Political Reorganization Committee, and Wang Kemin, the newly appointed Chief Advisor of the Tianjin Political Reorganization Committee and Mayor of Tianjin, are still in Shanghai and have no plans to return north. According to Xin Sheng News reporters, although both are staying in Shanghai, they continue to direct and handle North China political affairs through letters and telegrams, and there are frequent telecommunications between Tianjin, Beijing, and Chongqing. Beiping Mayor Yuan Liang telegraphed Huang Fu yesterday, reporting that peace and tranquility in Beiping is as usual and people are not afraid.

Today's Memorial: Premier's Guangzhou Assassination; Municipal Party Headquarters Meeting; Citywide Half-Mast Flag 156

Today is the 13th anniversary of the Premier's assassination in Guangzhou. The Municipal Party Headquarters has designated 9:00 AM this morning to hold a memorial meeting at the Party Headquarters Auditorium on Fenglin Bridge, and has appointed Standing Committee member Wu Xingya as the chairman of the meeting. The Party Headquarters has also notified all agencies, schools, and organizations to send two representatives each to attend the meeting. The city will fly flags at half-mast. Military and police agencies have stepped up security for the day, as it coincides with the revolutionary memorial.

Impending Drought in Municipal and County Four Suburbs; Locust Nymphs Discovered in Pudong and Nanhui 157

Da Gong News reports: The farmland in this city, including Shanghai South, Zhabei, Jiangwan, Pudong, Wusong, Zhenru, Guxing, Fahua, Pusong, Gaoxing, Yangsi, Gaoqiao, Yangjing, Yinxiang, Tangqiao, Caojing, Longhua, and other 17 districts, averages 40,000 mu per district, so the total farmland area of the city is approximately 680,000 mu. Among them, rice paddies account for 40%, cotton fields account for 50%, and other fields such as vegetable and fruit fields account for 10%. Cotton plants are growing unevenly due to the drought, with only about 30-40% growth per mu. Since sowing, the rice seedlings have been weak and fragile due to lack of rain. Although irrigated, the soil is cracked and withered under the scorching sun. The water in the ponds and swamps near the fields recedes several feet from the embankment during high tide and becomes shallow again after the tide recedes. If there is no heavy rainfall before the summer solstice, the disaster will be unavoidable.

Due to the prolonged drought in Pudong and Nanhui counties, the rice seedlings sown by farmers are growing on dry land. In addition, the hot weather has led to the discovery of locust nymphs densely populating the fields. After the farmers reported to the county government, they were instructed to order farmers in the four suburbs to dig trenches to drive the locust nymphs into the trenches and drown or burn them. According to the county government's investigation, the number of locust nymphs in each township reached more than 200 dan. Fortunately, they were discovered early, and the rice seedlings have not yet suffered a major attack.

Japanese Ambassador Returned to Shanghai Yesterday 158

Central News Agency reports that the first Japanese Ambassador to China, Akira Ariyoshi, accompanied by Counselor Horiuchi, Arino, Yokotake, Yamada, Military Attaché Sato, and Secretary Yokokawa of the embassy, entered Beijing on the morning of the 13th. On the 14th, he met with Chairman Lin of the National Government to present his credentials and visited the Premier's Mausoleum to lay flowers and pay his respects. He completed his official duties and arrived in Shanghai by overnight express train from Beijing at 7:15 AM yesterday. The Municipal Security Department and the Municipal Public Security Bureau deployed guards around the station to provide security. Municipal Government Commissioner Wang Changchun, Japanese Consul General to Shanghai Ishii, Director of the Information Office Ashino, Commander of the Third Japanese Fleet to China Vice Admiral Araki, Commander of the Japanese Naval Landing Force in Shanghai Sugiaka, and others were present at the station to welcome him. After getting off the train, he returned to his private residence on Huaxun Road to rest. As for the second Japanese Consuls General Conference in China, it is scheduled to be held in Shanghai on the 25th of this month. Japanese Consul General to Guangzhou Kawai, Consul General to Beijing Suma, and Consuls General stationed in Tianjin, Jinan, and other places will depart for Shanghai before the meeting to participate. It is reported that the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs has also decided to send personnel to attend the meeting as observers. Ambassador Ariyoshi will depart for Beiping after the conference to handle embassy affairs.
